   Carakasaṃhitā, Sūtrasthāna, 1	Caraka saMhitA, SUtra sTAna, 1
   athāto dīrghaṃjīvitīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ // Car_1,1.1	aTa atas dIrGaMjIvitIyam aDyAyam vyAKyAsyAmaH // Car_1,1.1
   [{Āyurvedadīpikā}	[{Āyurveda dIpikA}
   guṇatrayavibhedena mūrtitrayam upaiyuṣe /	guNatraya viBedena mUrti trayam upEyuze /
   trayībhuve trinetrāya trilokīpataye namaḥ // 1	trayI Buve trinetrAya trilokI pataye namaH // 1
   sarasvatyai namo yasyāḥ prasādāt puṇyakarmabhiḥ /	sarasvatyE namaH yasyAH prasAdAt puNya karmaBiH /
   buddhidarpaṇasaṃkrāntaṃ jagadadhyakṣam īkṣyate // 2	budDi darpaNa saMkrAntam jagat aDyakzam Ikzyate // 2
   brahmadakṣāśvideveśabharadvājapunarvasu	brahma dakza aSvideveSa BaradvAja punarvasu
   hutāśaveśacarakaprabhṛtibhyo namo namaḥ // 3	hutASa veSa caraka praBRtiByaH namaH namaH // 3

   naradattagurūddiṣṭacarakārthānugāminī /	naradatta guru uddizwa caraka arTa anugAminI /
   kriyate cakradattena ṭīkāyurvedadīpikā // 5	kriyate cakradattena wIkA Ayurveda dIpikA // 5
   sabhyāḥ sadguruvāksudhāsrutiparisphītaśrutīn asmi vo nālaṃ toṣayituṃ	saByAH sat guru vAc suDA sruti parisPIta SrutIn asmi vaH na alam tozayitum
   payodapayasā nāmbhonidhis tṛpyati /	payoda payasA na amBoniDiH tRpyati /
   vyākhyābhāsarasaprakāśanam idaṃ tv asmin yadi prāpyate kvāpi kvāpi kaṇo	vyAKyA BAsa rasa prakASanam idam tu asmin yadi prApyate kvApi kvApi kaNaH 
   guṇasya tadasau karṇe kṣaṇaṃ dhīyatām // 6	guNasya tat asO karNe kzaNam DIyatAm // 6
   iha hi dharmārthakāmamokṣaparipanthirogopaśamāya brahmaprabhṛtibhiḥ	iha hi Darma arTa kAma mokza paripanTi roga upaSamAya brahma praBRtiBiH
   praṇītāyurvedatantreṣvativistaratvena samprati vartamānālpāyurmedhasāṃ	praNIta Ayurveda tantrezu ati vistara tvena samprati vartamAna alpa AyuH meDasAm
   puruṣāṇāṃ na samyagarthādhigamaḥ tadanadhigamācca	puruzANAm na samyak arTa aDigamaH tad anaDigamAt ca
   tadvihitārthānāmananuṣṭhāne tathaivopaplavo rujāmiti manvānaḥ	tad vihita arTAnAm ananuzWAne taTA eva upaplavaH rujAm iti manvAnaH
   paramakāruṇiko 'trabhavān agniveśo'lpāyurmedhasāmapi suropalambhārthaṃ	parama kAruNikaH atraBavAn agniveSaH alpa AyuH meDasAm api sura upalamBa arTam
   nātisaṃkṣepavistaraṃ kāyacikitsāpradhānam āyurvedatantraṃ praṇetum	na ati saMkzepa vistaram kAya cikitsA praDAnam Ayurveda tantram praNetum
   ārabdhavān // 7	ArabDavAn // 7
   tasmiṃśca ślokanidānavimānaśārīrendriyacikitsitakalpasiddhisthānātmake	tasmin= ca Sloka nidAna vimAna SArIra indriya cikitsita kalpa sidDi sTAna Atmake
   'bhidhātavye nikhilatantrapradhānārthābhidhāya // 8	aBiDAtavye niKila tantra praDAna arTa aBiDAya // 8
   ktā ityādivākyābhidhāyakena darśitaṃ mantavyam // 9	ktA ityAdi vAkya aBiDAyakena darSitam mantavyam // 9
   nanu prayojanābhidhānaṃ śāstrapravṛttyarthamiti yaduktaṃ tanna yuktaṃ yato	nanu prayojana aBiDAnam SAstra pravRtti arTam iti yat uktam tat na yuktam yatas 
   na prayojanābhidhānamātreṇa prayojanavattāvadhāraṇaṃ	na prayojana aBiDAna mAtreNa prayojanavat tA avaDAraNam
   vipralambhakasaṃsāramocanapratipādakādiśāstreṣu prayojanābhidhāne'pi	vipralamBaka saMsAra mocana pratipAdaka Adi SAstrezu prayojana aBiDAne api
   niṣprayojanatvadarśanāt // 10	nizprayojana tva darSanAt // 10
   atha manyase āptaprayojanābhidhānametadato'tra yathārthatvaṃ nanu bho	aTa manyase Apta prayojana aBiDAnam etat atas atra yaTArTa tvam nanu Bo
   kathamayaṃ prayojanābhidhāyī āptaḥ tadabhihitaśāstrasya yathārthatvāditi	kaTam ayam prayojana aBiDAyI AptaH tad aBihita SAstrasya yaTArTa tvAt iti
   cet hanta na yāvacchāstrasya prayojanavattāvadhāraṇaṃ na	ced hanta na yAvat SAstrasya prayojanavat tA avaDAraNam na
   tāvacchāstrapravṛttiḥ na yāvacchāstrapravṛttir na tāvacchāstrasya	tAvat SAstra pravRttiH na yAvat SAstra pravRttiH na tAvat SAstrasya
   yathārthatvāvadhāraṇaṃ na yāvacchāstrasya yathārthatvāvadhāraṇaṃ na	yaTArTa tva avaDAraNam na yAvat SAstrasya yaTArTa tva avaDAraNam na
   tāvacchāstrasya karturāptatvamavadhāryate āptatvānavadhṛtau ca kutas	tAvat SAstrasya kartuH Apta tvam avaDAryate Apta tva anavaDRtO ca kutas 
   tadabhihitaprayojanavattāvadhāraṇam iti cakrakamāpadyate atha manyase mā	tad aBihita prayojanavattA avaDAraNam iti cakrakam Apadyate aTa manyase mA
   bhavatu prayojanavattāvadhāraṇam artharūpaprayojanavattāsaṃdeha eva	Bavatu prayojanavat tA avaDAraNam arTa rUpa prayojana vat tA saMdehaH eva
   pravartako bhaviṣyati kṛṣyādāv api hi pravṛttir arthasaṃdehādeva na hi	pravartakaH Bavizyati kRzi AdO api hi pravRttiH arTa saMdehAt eva na hi
   tatra kṛṣīvalānāṃ phalalābhāvadhāraṇaṃ vidyate	tatra kRzIvalAnAm Pala lABa avaDAraNam vidyate
   antarāvagrahāderapisaṃbhāvyamānatvāt nanvevamasatyapi prayojanābhidhāne	antarA avagraha AdeH apisaMBAvyamAna tvAt nanu evam asati api prayojana aBiDAne
   saprayojananiṣprayojanaśāstradarśanācchāstratvam eva	sa prayojana nizprayojana SAstra darSanAt SAstra tvam eva
   prayojanavattāsaṃdehopadarśakam astu tathāpyalaṃ prayojanābhidhānena // 11	prayojana vat tA saMdeha upadarSakam astu taTA api alam prayojana aBiDAnena // 11
   naivaṃ nahi sāmānyena prayojanasaṃdehaḥ prayojanaviśeṣārthinaṃ tathā	na evam na hi sAmAnyena prayojana saMdehaH prayojana viSeza arTinam taTA
   pravartayati yathābhipretaprayojanaviśeṣaviṣayaḥ saṃdehaḥ	pravartayati yaTA aBipreta prayojana viSeza vizayaH saMdehaH
   abhipretaviśeṣaviṣayaśca saṃdeho na viśeṣaviṣayasmaraṇamantarā bhavati ato	aBipreta viSeza vizayaH ca saMdehaH na viSeza vizaya smaraNam antarA Bavati atas 
   ye tāvad anavadhṛtāgniveśaprāmāṇyās teṣāṃ dhātusāmyasādhanamidaṃ śāstraṃ	ye tAvat anavaDRta agniveSa prAmANyAH tezAm DAtu sAmya sADanam idam SAstram
   na vetyevam ākāraviśeṣasaṃdehotpādanārthaṃ prayojanaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ ye	na vA iti evam AkAra viSeza saMdeha utpAdana arTam prayojana viSeza aBiDAnam ye
   punaḥ paramarṣeragniveśasyādyata evāvadhṛtaprāmāṇyāsteṣāṃ	punar parama RzeH agniveSasya adyataH eva avaDRta prAmANyAH tezAm
   tadabhihitaprayojanavattāvadhāraṇenaiva pravṛttir iti yuktaṃ	tad aBihita prayojana vattA avaDAraNena eva pravRttiH iti yuktam
   prayojanābhidhānam // 12	prayojana aBiDAnam // 12
   prayojanābhidhāyivākye tu svalpaprayatnabodhye prayojanasāmānyasaṃdehādeva	prayojana aBiDAyi vAkye tu su alpa prayatna boDye prayojana sAmAnya saMdehAt eva
   pravṛttirupapannā na punaranekasaṃvatsarakleśabodhye śāstre // 13	pravRttiH upapannAH na punar aneka saMvatsara kleSa boDye SAstre // 13
   tadevaṃ yaducyate prayojanābhidhāyivākyapravṛttāv api	tat evam yat ucyate prayojana aBiDAyi vAkya pravRttO api
   prayojanamabhidhātavyaṃ tathā cānavasthā iti tannirastaṃ bhavati // 14	prayojanam aBiDAtavyam taTA ca anavasTA iti tat nirastam Bavati // 14
   athetyādi sūtre 'thaśabdo brahmādipraṇītatantreṣv	aTa ityAdi sUtre aTa SabdaH brahma Adi praNIta tantrezu 
   alpāyurmedhasāmarthānavadhāraṇasya	alpa AyuH meDasAm arTAn avaDAraNasya
   tathābhīṣṭadevatānamaskāraśāstrakaraṇārthagurvājñālābhayor ānantarye	taTA aBIzwa devatA namaskAra SAstra karaNa arTa guru AjQAla ABayoH Anantarye
   prayukto'pi śāstrādau svarūpeṇa maṅgalaṃ	prayuktaH api SAstra AdO svarUpeNa maFgalam
   bhavatyudakāharaṇapravṛttodakumbhadarśanam iva prasthitānām // 15	Bavati udaka AharaNa pravRttoda kumBa darSanam iva prasTitAnAm // 15
   granthādau maṅgalasevānirastāntarāyāṇāṃ granthakartṛśrotḥṇām	granTa AdO maFgala sevA nirasta antarAyANAm granTa kartR SrotHNAm
   avighneneṣṭalābho bhavatīti yuktaṃ maṅgalopādānam // 16	aviGnena izwa lABaH Bavati iti yuktam maFgala upAdAnam // 16
   athaśabdasya maṅgalatve smṛtir oṃkāraś cāthaśabdaśca dvāv etau brahmaṇaḥ	aTaSabdasya maFgala tve smRtiH oMkAraH ca aTa SabdaH ca dvO etO brahmaNaH
   purā // 17	purA // 17
   kaṇṭhaṃ bhittvā viniryātau tena māṅgalikāv ubhau iti // 18	kaNWam BittvA viniryAtO tena mAFgalikO uBO iti // 18
   śāstrāntare cādau maṅgalatvena dṛṣṭo'yamathaśabdaḥ // 19	SAstra antare ca AdO maFgala tvena dRzwaH ayam aTa SabdaH // 19
   yathā atha śabdānuśāsanam athāto dharmaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ vai ityādau // 20	yaTA aTa Sabda anuSAsanam aTa atas Darmam vyAKyAsyAmaH vE ityAdO // 20
   abhīṣṭadevatānamaskārastu granthādau śiṣṭācāraprāptaḥ	aBIzwa devatA namaskAraH tu granTa AdO Sizwa AcAra prAptaH
   paramaśiṣṭenāgniveśena kṛta eva anyathā śiṣṭācāralaṅghanena śiṣṭatvameva	parama Sizwena agniveSena kRtaH eva anyaTA Sizwa AcAra laFGanena Sizwa tvam eva
   na syād vyākhyānāntarāyabhayaśca tathā granthāviniveśitasyāpi namaskārasya	na syAt vyAKyAna antarAya BayaH ca taTA granTa aviniveSitasya api namaskArasya
   pratyavāyāpahatvācca na granthaniveśanam // 21	pratyavAya apaha tvAt ca na granTa niveSanam // 21
   yathā ca gurvājñālābhānantaram etat tantrakaraṇaṃ tathā atha maitrīparaḥ	yaTA ca guru AjQAla aBa anantaram etat tantra karaNam taTA aTa mEtrI paraH
   puṇyam ityādau sphuṭameva // 22	puNyam ityAdO sPuwam eva // 22

   bhavati // 23	Bavati // 23
   yat punaḥ śiṣyapraśnānantaryārthatvam athaśabdasya varṇyate tanna māṃ	yat punar Sizya praSna Anantarya arTa tvam aTa Sabdasya varNyate tat na mAm
   dhinoti nahi śiṣyān puro vyavasthāpya śāstraṃ kriyate śrotṛbuddhisthīkāre	Dinoti na hi SizyAn puras vyavasTApya SAstram kriyate SrotR budDi sTIkAre
   tu śāstrakaraṇaṃ yuktaṃ na ca buddhisthīkṛtāḥ praṣṭāro bhavanti // 24	tu SAstra karaNam yuktam na ca budDi sTIkRtAH prazwAraH Bavanti // 24
   ataḥśabdo 'dhikāraprāgavadhyupadarśakaḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ yad upadekṣyāmo	atas SabdaH aDikAra prAc avaDi upadarSakaH atas UrDvam yat upadekzyAmaH 
   dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ taditi yadi vā hetau yena brahmādipraṇītāyurvedatantrāṇām	dIrGaMjIvitIyam tat iti yadi vA hetO yena brahma Adi praNIta Ayurveda tantrANAm
   uktena nyāyenotsambandhatvam iva ato hetor dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma	uktena nyAyena utsambanDa tvam iva atas hetoH dIrGaMjIvitIyam vyAKyAsyAma
   iti yojanīyam // 25	iti yojanIyam // 25
   dīrghaṃjīvitīyam ityatra dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdo 'sminn astīti matvarthe	dIrGaMjIvitIyam iti atra dIrGaMjIvita SabdaH asmin asti iti matu arTe
   adhyāyānuvākayor luk ca iti chapratyayaḥ // 26	aDyAya anuvAkayoH luc ca iti CapratyayaH // 26
   yadi vā dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdam adhikṛtya kṛto grantho 'dhyāyarūpastantrarūpo	yadi vA dIrGaMjIvita Sabdam aDikRtya kRtaH granTaH aDyAya rUpaH tantra rUpaH 
   vā ityasyāṃ vivakṣāyām adhikṛtya kṛte granthe ityadhikārāt	vA iti asyAm vivakzAyAm aDikRtya kRte granTe iti aDikArAt
   śiśukrandayamasabha ityādinā chaḥ // 27	SiSu krandayama saBaH ityAdinA CaH // 27
   evamanyatrāpyevaṃjātīye mantavyam // 28	evam anyatra api evaMjAtIye mantavyam // 28

   dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdasyaiva pravacanādau niveśāt praśastatvācca // 29	dIrGaMjIvita Sabdasya eva pravacana AdO niveSAt praSasta tvAt ca // 29
   dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdo 'sminn asti iti dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdam adhikṛtya kṛto vā	dIrGaMjIvita SabdaH asmin asti iti dIrGaMjIvita Sabdam aDikRtya kRtaH vA
   ityanayā vyutpattyā dīrghaṃjīvitīyaśabdas tantre 'dhyāye ca pravartanīyaḥ	iti anayA vyutpattyA dIrGaMjIvitIya SabdaH tantre aDyAye ca pravartanIyaH
   tena dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ityanena tantraṃ prati	tena dIrGaMjIvitIyam vyAKyAsyAmaH iti anena tantram prati
   vyākhyānapratijñā labdhā bhavati punar dīrghaṃjīvitīyam iti padam	vyAKyAna pratijQA labDA Bavati punar dIrGaMjIvitIyam iti padam
   āvartyādhyāyapadasamabhivyāhṛtam adhyāyavyākhyānapratijñāṃ lambhayati //	Avartya aDyAya pada samaBivyAhRtam aDyAya vyAKyAna pratijQAm lamBayati //
   dṛṣṭaṃ cāvṛtya padasya yojanaṃ yathā apāmārgataṇḍulīye gaurave śirasaḥ	dRzwam ca AvRtya padasya yojanam yaTA apAmArga taNxulIye gOrave SirasaH
   śūle pīnase ityādau śirasa iti padaṃ gaurave ityanena yujyate āvṛtya śūle	SUle pInase iti AdO SirasaH iti padam gOrave iti anena yujyate AvRtya SUle
   ityanena ca // 32	iti anena ca // 32
   ataśca yaducyate akṛtatantrapratijñasyādhyāyapratijñā ūnakāyamāneti	atas ca yat ucyate akRta tantra pratijQasya aDyAya pratijQA Una kAyamAnA iti
   tannirastaṃ bhavati // 33	tat nirastam Bavati // 33
   yadi vā adhyāyapratijñaivāstu tayaiva tantrapratijñāpyarthalabdhaiva na hy	yadi vE aDyAya pratijQA eva astu tayA eva tantra pratijQA api arTa labDA eva na hi 
   adhyāyas tantravyatiriktaḥ tenāvayavavyākhyāne tantrasyāpyavayavino	aDyAyaH tantra vyatiriktaH tena avayava vyAKyAne tantrasya api avayavinaH 
   vyākhyā bhavatyeva yathā aṅgulīgrahaṇena devadatto'pi gṛhīto bhavati // 34	vyAKyA Bavati eva yaTA aFgulI grahaNena devadattaH api gRhItaH Bavati // 34
   avayavāntaravyākhyānapratijñā tu na labhyate tāṃ tu pratyadhyāyameva	avayava antara vyAKyAna pratijQA tu na laByate tAm tu pratyaDyAyam eva
   kariṣyati // 35	karizyati // 35
   adhyāyamiti adhipūrvādiṅaḥ iṅaśca iti karmaṇi ghañā sādhyam // 36	aDyAyam iti aDipUrva AdiFaH iFaH ca iti karmaNi GaQA sADyam // 36
   tena adhīyate ityadhyāyaḥ // 37	tena aDIyate iti aDyAyaH // 37
   na cānayā vyutpattyā prakaraṇacatuṣkasthānādiṣvatiprasaṅgaḥ yato	na ca anayA vyutpattyA prakaraNa catuzka sTAna Adizu atiprasaFgaH yatas 
   yogarūḍheyam adhyāyasaṃjñādhyāyasya prakaraṇasamūhaviśeṣa eva	yoga rUXA iyam aDyAya saMjQA DyAyasya prakaraNa samUha viSezaH eva
   dīrghaṃjīvitīyādilakṣaṇe paṅkajaśabdavadvartate na yogamātreṇa vartate //	dIrGaMjIvitIya Adi lakzaNe paFkaja Sabda vat vartate na yoga mAtreNa vartate //
   vakṣyati hi adhikṛtyeyamadhyāyanāmasaṃjñā pratiṣṭhitā iti nāmasaṃjñā	vakzyati hi aDikRtya iyam aDyAya nAma saMjQA pratizWitAH iti nAma saMjQA
   yogarūḍhasaṃjñetyarthaḥ // 39	yoga rUXa saMjQA ityarTaH // 39
   yadi vā karaṇādhikaraṇayor arthayoḥ // 40	yadi vA karaNa aDikaraNayoH arTayoH // 40
   adhyāyanyāyodyāvasaṃhārāś ca itisūtreṇa nipātanād adhyāyapadasiddhiḥ // 41	aDyAya nyAya udyAva saMhArAH ca iti sUtreNa nipAtanAt aDyAya pada sidDiH // 41

   cakṣiṅo hi prayoge'nicchato 'pi vyākhyātuḥ kriyāphalasambandhasya	cakziFaH hi prayoge anicCataH api vyAKyAtuH kriyA Pala sambanDasya
   durnivāratvena svaritañita ityādinātmanepadaṃ syāditi // 45	durnivAra tvena svaritaQitaH ityAdinA Atmanepadam syAt iti // 45
   vi iti viśeṣe viśeṣāśca vyāsasamāsādayaḥ // 46	vi iti viSeze viSezAH ca vyAsa samAsa AdayaH // 46
   āṅayaṃ kriyāyoge ye tu maryādāyām abhividhau vā āṅprayogaṃ manyante teṣām	AFayam kriyA yoge ye tu maryAdAyAm aBiviDO vE AFprayogam manyante tezAm
   abhiprāyaṃ na vidmaḥ // 47	aBiprAyam na vidmaH // 47
   yato maryādāyāmabhividhau cāṅaḥ prātipadikena yogaḥ syāt yathā	yatas maryAdAyAm aBiviDO ca aFaH prAtipadikena yogaH syAt yaTA
   āsamudrakṣitīśānām āpāṭalīputrād vṛṣṭo deva ityādau ihāpi ca tathā // 48	Asamudra kzitISAnAm ApAwalI putrAt vRzwaH devaH ityAdO iha api ca taTA // 48
   kriyāyogavirahe upasargāḥ kriyāyoge iti niyamād āṅa upasargatvaṃ na syāt	kriyA yoga virahe upasargAH kriyA yoge iti niyamAt AFaH upasarga tvam na syAt 
   tataścānupasargeṇāṅā vyavadhānād ver upasargasya prayogo na syāt // 49	tatas ca anupasargeNa AFA vyavaDAnAt veH upasargasya prayogaH na syAt // 49
   yenāvyavahitaḥ sajātīyavyavahito vā dhātor upasargo bhavati // 50	yena avyavahitaH sajAtIya vyavahitaH vA DAtoH upasargaH Bavati // 50

   yoniḥ ādhārakāraṇaṃ kāryakāraṇayośca bhedāt siddha udakādrasabhedaḥ	yoniH ADAra kAraNam kArya kAraNayoH ca BedAt sidDaH udakAt rasa BedaH

   madhuram ityādi // 1	maDuram ityAdi // 1

   raukṣyād ityādi // 1	rOkzyAt ityAdi // 1

   samprati vipākasyāpi rasarūpatvāllakṣaṇam āha paramityādi // 1	samprati vipAkasya api rasa rUpa tvAt lakzaNam Aha param ityAdi // 1

   pittaraktādikārakaṃ vipākastu tatra pittaraktaharaṇalakṣaṇe kārye bādhitaḥ	pitta rakta Adi kArakam vipAkaH tu tatra pitta rakta haraNa lakzaNe kArye bADitaH

   [{Āyurvedadīpikā}	[{Āyurveda dIpikA}
   ayanāni ca tāni mukhāni cetyayanamukhāni atra āyāntyanenetyayanāni mārgāṇi	ayanAni ca tAni muKAni ca iti ayana muKAni atra AyAnti anena iti ayanAni mArgANi

   praveśamukhamiti nānyena praveśo nānyena ca gamanam ityuktaṃ bhavati // 1	praveSa muKam iti na anyena praveSaH na anyena ca gamanam iti uktam Bavati // 1

   [{Āyurvedadīpikā}	[{Āyurveda dIpikA}
   dṛśyante hi bhagavannityādau tathaivāhitasamākhyātam upayuñjānā	dRSyante hi Bagavan= ityAdO taTA eva ahita samAKyAtam upayuQjAnA
   vyādhimantaś cāgadāśceti sambandhaḥ // 1	vyADimantaH ca agadAH ca iti sambanDaH // 1

   sampadyate /	sampadyate /
   sa eva doṣa saṃsṛṣṭayonirviruddhopakramo gambhīrānugataś cirasthitaḥ	saH eva doza saMsRzwa yoniH virudDa upakramaH gamBIra anugataH cira sTitaH
   prāṇāyatanasamuttho marmopaghātī kaṣṭatamaḥ kṣiprakāritamaśca sampadyate /	prANa Ayatana samutTaH marma upaGAtI kazwatamaH kziprakAritamaH ca sampadyate /
